191→func (mg *Migrator) RunMigrations(ctx context.Context, isDatabaseLockingEnabled bool, lockAttemptTimeout int) (err error) {\n   192→\tif !isDatabaseLockingEnabled {\n   193→\t\treturn 232→\n   233→func (mg *Migrator) run(ctx context.Context) (err error) {\n   234→\tctx, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"Migrator.run\")\n   235→\tdefer span.End()\n   236→\n   237→\tlogger := mg.Logger.FromContext(ctx)\n   238→\n   239→\tlogger.Info(\"Starting DB migrations\")\n   240→\n   241→\tmigrationLogExists, err := mg.DBEngine.IsTableExist(mg.tableName)\n   242→\tif err != nil {\n   243→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to check table existence: %w\", err)\n   244→\t}\n   245→\n   246→\tif !migrationLogExists {\n   247→\t\t// Check if dialect can initialize database from a 262→\t\t\treturn err\n   263→\t\t}\n   264→\t}\n   265→\n   266→\tsuccessLabel := prometheus.Labels{\"success\": \"true\"}\n   267→\n   268→\tmigrationsPerformed := 0\n   269→\tmigrationsSkipped := 0\n   270→\tstart := time.Now()\n   271→\tfor _, m := range mg.migrations {\n   272→\t\t_, exists := mg.logMap[m.Id()]\n   273→\t\tif exists {\n   274→\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Skipping migration: Already 278→\t\t\tmigrationsSkipped++\n   279→\t\t\tcontinue\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\n   282→\t\tmigStart := time.Now()\n   283→\n   284→\t\tif err := mg.doMigration(ctx, m); err != nil {\n   285→\t\t\tfailLabel := prometheus.Labels{\"success\": \"false\"}\n   286→\t\t\tmetricutil.ObserveWithExemplar(ctx, mg.metrics.migDuration.With(failLabel), time.Since(migStart).Seconds())\n   287→\t\t\tmg.metrics.migCount.With(failLabel).Inc()\n   288→\t\t\treturn err\n   289→\t\t}\n   290→\n   291→\t\tmetricutil.ObserveWithExemplar(ctx, mg.metrics.migDuration.With(successLabel), doMigration(ctx context.Context, m Migration) error {\n   306→\tctx, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"Migrator.doMigration\", trace.WithAttributes(\n   307→\t\tattribute.String(\"migration_id\", m.Id()),\n   308→\t))\n   309→\tdefer span.End()\n   310→\n   311→\tlogger := mg.Logger.FromContext(ctx)\n   312→\n   313→\tsql := m.SQL(mg.Dialect)\n   314→\n   315→\trecord := MigrationLog{\n   316→\t\tMigrationID: m.Id(),\n   317→\t\tSQL:         sql,\n   318→\t\tTimestamp:   time.Now(),\n   319→\t}\n   320→\n   321→\terr := mg.InTransaction(func(sess *xorm.Session) error {\n   322→\t\t// := 0\n   328→\t\tfor cnt < 3 && sqlite.IsBusyOrLocked(err) {\n   329→\t\t\tcnt++\n   330→\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Database locked, sleeping then retrying\", \"error\", err, \"sql\", sql)\n   331→\t\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Database locked, sleeping then retrying\",\n   332→\t\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(attribute.String(\"error\", err.Error())),\n   333→\t\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(attribute.String(\"sql\", sql)),\n   334→\t\t\t)\n   335→\t\t\ttime.Sleep(100 * time.Millisecond)\n   336→\t\t\terr = mg.exec(ctx, m, sess)\n   337→\t\t}\n   338→\n   339→\t\tif err != nil {\n   340→\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"Exec failed\", \"error\", err, \"sql\", sql)\n   341→\t\t\trecord.Error = err.Error()\n   342→\t\t\tif !m.SkipMigrationLog() {\n   343→\t\t\t\tif _, err := sess.Table(mg.tableName).Insert(&record); err != nil {\n   344→\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n   345→\t\t\t\t}\n   346→\t\t\t}\n   347→\t\t\treturn err\n   348→\t\t}\n   349→\t\trecord.Success = true\n   350→\t\tif !m.SkipMigrationLog() {\n   351→\t\t\t_, err = sess.Table(mg.tableName).Insert(&record)\n   352→\t\t}\n   353→\t\treturn err\n   354→\t})\n   355→\tif err != nil {\n   356→\t\treturn tracing.Errorf(span, \"migration failed (id = %s): %w\", m.Id(), err)\n   357→\t}\n   358→\n   359→\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Ok, \"\")\n   360→\n   361→\treturn nil\n   362→}\n   363→\n   364→func (mg *Migrator) exec(ctx context.Context, m Migration, sess *xorm.Session) error {\n   365→\tlogger := mg.Logger.FromContext(ctx)\n   366→\n   367→\tstart := time.Now()\n   368→\tlogger.Info(\"Executing migration\", \"id\", m.Id())\n   369→\n   370→\tcondition := m.GetCondition()\n   371→\tif condition != nil {\n   372→\t\tsql, args := condition.SQL(mg.Dialect)\n   373→\n   374→\t\tif sql != \"\" {\n   375→\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Executing migration condition SQL\", \"id\", m.Id(), \"sql\", sql, \"args\", args)\n   376→\t\t\tresults, err := sess.SQL(sql, args...).Query()\n   377→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   378→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"Executing migration condition failed\", \"id\", m.Id(), \"error\", err)\n   379→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   380→\t\t\t}\n   381→\n   382→\t\t\tif !condition.IsFulfilled(results) {\n   383→\t\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"Skipping migration: Already executed, but not recorded in migration log\", \"id\", m.Id())\n   384→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   385→\t\t\t}\n   386→\t\t}\n   387→\t}\n   388→\n   389→\tvar err error\n   390→\tif codeMigration, ok := m.(CodeMigration); ok {\n   391→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Executing code migration\", \"id\", empty sql migration\", \"id\", m.Id())\n   397→\t\t} else {\n   398→\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Executing sql migration\", \"id\", m.Id(), \"sql\", sql)\n   399→\t\t\t_, err = sess.Exec(sql)\n   400→\t\t}\n 406→\t}\n   407→\n   408→\tlogger.Info(\"Migration successfully executed\", \"id\", m.Id(), \"duration\", time.Since(start))\n   409→\n   410→\treturn nil\n   411→}\n   412→\n   413→type dbTransactionFunc func(sess *xorm.Session) error\n   414→\n   415→func (mg *Migrator) InTransaction(callback dbTransactionFunc) error {\n   416→\tsess := mg.DBEngine.NewSession()\n   417→\tdefer sess.Close()\n   418→\n   419→\tif err := sess.Begin(); err != nil {\n   420→\t\treturn err\n   421→\t}\n   422→\n   423→\tif err := callback(sess); err != nil {\n   424→\t\tif rollErr := sess.Rollback(); rollErr != nil {\n   425→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to roll back transaction due to error: %s: %w\", rollErr, err)\n   426→\t\t}\n   427→\n   428→\t\treturn err\n   429→\t}\n   430→\n   431→\tif err := sess.Commit(); err != nil {\n   432→\t\treturn err\n   433→\t}\n   434→\n   435→\treturn nil\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→func casRestoreOnErr(lock *atomic.Bool, o, n bool,
